NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
J. Vasanthakumar, a male Child, born to T. Jeganathan on 4th May 1990, residing at No. 67, East Street,
Nadukuppam Post, Panruti Taluk, Cuddalore-607 103, has been living as a female after an elaborate Sexual Reassignment
on 22nd May, 2015 at Kilpauk Medical College Hospital, Chennai-600 010, surgery by Dr. V. Jayaraman, Former Professor
and Head, Department of Burns, Plastic & Reconstructive surgery, Kilpauk Medical College Hospital, Chennai-600 010,
(Reg. No. 32070). By this I may be treated as a female and shall henceforth be known as Ms. J. KAVIYA.
Cuddalore,
20th September 2016.

J. VASANTHAKUMAR,

Jotheeswari, R., a female child born to Mr. P.V. Ramamoorthy on 13th March 1991 residing at No. 201N/180N,
5th Street, S.S.K. Nagar, Kancheepuram has been living as a Male after an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery by
Dr. Shivaram Bharathwaj, Reg. No. 40903, Dip.N.B. (Surg.), FRCS (Edin) FRCS (Plast.Surg), Apollo Speciality Hospital,
Chennai-600 035. By this I, may be treated as a male and shall henceforth be known as R. VISHWAA.
Kancheepuram,
22nd September 2016.

JOTHEESWARI, R.

N. Mageshkumar, a male child born to G. Nedunjezhian on 5th June 1989 residing at No. 32, Kamarajapuram
Extenstion, Nungambakkam, Chennai-600 034, has been living as a female after an elaborate sexual reassignment
surgery by Dr. V.B. Narayanamurthy from Sundaram Medical Foundation Hospital in Anna Nagar, 19th January 2012 by
this I, may be treated as a female and shall henceforth be known as N. JAYADEVI.
Chennai,
23rd September 2016.

N. MAGESHKUMAR.
